/* =============================================================================                                                                                
Program     : Severity_Formats.txt                                                                                                                              
Date Revised: 08/13/2018                                                                                                                                        
Descripiton :                                                                                                                                                   
Create SAS formats that may be used with SAS procedures to label the values of                                                                                  
data elements in the Severity File.  For example, the following SAS statements                                                                                  
use the APRDR34F format with the Freq Procedure to label the values of APRDRG in                                                                                
the frequency listing:                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                
    Proc Freq Data = NIS_2016_Severity ;                                                                                                                        
         Table APRDRG ;                                                                                                                                         
         Format APRDRG APRDR34F. ;                                                                                                                              
    Run ;                                                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                
The following tables list formats available for selected HCUP data elements.                                                                                    
(Note that some data elements are not always available.)                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                
    Severity File                                                                                                                                               
    Data Element(s)         Format Name(s)                                                                                                                      
    ===============         ==============                                                                                                                      
    APRDRG                  APRDRnnF. (where nn is the applicable APRDRG version number)                                                                        
    APRDRG_Risk_Mortality   FAPRDRGR.                                                                                                                           
    APRDRG_Severity         FAPRDRGS.                                                                                                                           
    APSDRG                  APSDRnnF. (where nn is the applicable APSDRG version number)                                                                        
    CM_AIDS                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_ALCOHOL              Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_ANEMDEF              Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_ARTH                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_BLDLOSS              Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_CHF                  Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_CHRNLUNG             Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_COAG                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_DEPRESS              Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_DM                   Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_DMCX                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_DRUG                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_HTN_C                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_HYPOTHY              Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_LIVER                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_LYMPH                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_LYTES                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_METS                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_NEURO                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_OBESE                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_PARA                 Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_PERIVASC             Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_PSYCH                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_PULMCIRC             Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_RENLFAIL             Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_TUMOR                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_ULCER                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_VALVE                Comor.                                                                                                                              
    CM_WGHTLOSS             Comor.                                                                                                                              
    DS_DX_Category1         $DXC5NTI.                                                                                                                           
    DS_LOS_Level            DSLOSLV.                                                                                                                            
    DS_Mrt_Level            DSMRTLV.                                                                                                                            
    DS_RD_Level             DSRDLV.                                                                                                                             
============================================================================= */
